**SLSA框架实施**

```yaml
# slsa-provenance.yaml - SLSA来源证明
apiVersion: v1
kind: ConfigMap
metadata:
  name: slsa-provenance
  namespace: ci-cd
data:
  provenance-template.json: |
    {
      "_type": "https://in-toto.io/Statement/v0.1",
      "predicateType": "https://slsa.dev/provenance/v0.2",
      "subject": [
        {
          "name": "registry.example.com/app",
          "digest": {
            "sha256": "<image-digest>"
          }
        }
      ],
      "predicate": {
        "builder": {
          "id": "https://github.com/org/repo/actions/runs/123456"
        },
        "buildType": "https://github.com/Attestations/GitHubActionsWorkflow@v1",
        "invocation": {
          "configSource": {
            "uri": "git+https://github.com/org/repo@refs/heads/main",
            "digest": {
              "sha1": "<commit-sha>"
            },
            "entryPoint": ".github/workflows/build.yml"
          },
          "parameters": {},
          "environment": {
            "github_actor": "user",
            "github_sha": "<commit-sha>",
            "github_event_name": "push"
          }
        },
        "buildConfig": {
          "steps": [
            {
              "command": ["docker", "build", "-t", "app:latest", "."],
              "env": []
            }
          ]
        },
        "metadata": {
          "buildInvocationId": "123456",
          "buildStartedOn": "2024-01-01T00:00:00Z",
          "buildFinishedOn": "2024-01-01T00:10:00Z",
          "completeness": {
            "parameters": true,
            "environment": true,
            "materials": true
          },
          "reproducible": false
        },
        "materials": [
          {
            "uri": "git+https://github.com/org/repo@refs/heads/main",
            "digest": {
              "sha1": "<commit-sha>"
            }
          }
        ]
      }
    }
```

**GitHub Actions安全构建**

```yaml
# .github/workflows/secure-build.yml
name: Secure Build and Push

on:
  push:
    branches: [ main ]
  pull_request:
    branches: [ main ]

permissions:
  contents: read
  packages: write
  id-token: write  # 用于Sigstore签名

jobs:
  build:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
    - name: Checkout code
      uses: actions/checkout@v3
      with:
        fetch-depth: 0  # 完整历史用于SBOM生成
    
    - name: Set up Docker Buildx
      uses: docker/setup-buildx-action@v2
    
    - name: Log in to Container Registry
      uses: docker/login-action@v2
      with:
        registry: ghcr.io
        username: ${{ github.actor }}
        password: ${{ secrets.GITHUB_TOKEN }}
    
    # 依赖扫描
    - name: Run dependency scan
      uses: aquasecurity/trivy-action@master
      with:
        scan-type: 'fs'
        scan-ref: '.'
        format: 'sarif'
        output: 'trivy-results.sarif'
    
    # 构建镜像
    - name: Build image
      uses: docker/build-push-action@v4
      with:
        context: .
        push: false
        load: true
        tags: ghcr.io/${{ github.repository }}:${{ github.sha }}
        cache-from: type=gha
        cache-to: type=gha,mode=max
    
    # 镜像扫描
    - name: Scan image
      uses: aquasecurity/trivy-action@master
      with:
        image-ref: ghcr.io/${{ github.repository }}:${{ github.sha }}
        format: 'sarif'
        output: 'trivy-image-results.sarif'
        exit-code: '1'
        severity: 'CRITICAL,HIGH'
    
    # 生成SBOM
    - name: Generate SBOM
      uses: anchore/sbom-action@v0
      with:
        image: ghcr.io/${{ github.repository }}:${{ github.sha }}
        format: spdx-json
        output-file: sbom.spdx.json
    
    # 推送镜像
    - name: Push image
      uses: docker/build-push-action@v4
      with:
        context: .
        push: true
        tags: |
          ghcr.io/${{ github.repository }}:${{ github.sha }}
          ghcr.io/${{ github.repository }}:latest
    
    # 使用Cosign签名(Keyless)
    - name: Install Cosign
      uses: sigstore/cosign-installer@v3
    
    - name: Sign image
      run: |
        cosign sign --yes \
          ghcr.io/${{ github.repository }}:${{ github.sha }}
    
    # 附加SBOM到镜像
    - name: Attach SBOM
      run: |
        cosign attach sbom --sbom sbom.spdx.json \
          ghcr.io/${{ github.repository }}:${{ github.sha }}
    
    # 生成SLSA来源证明
    - name: Generate provenance
      uses: slsa-framework/slsa-github-generator/.github/workflows/generator_container_slsa3.yml@v1.5.0
      with:
        image: ghcr.io/${{ github.repository }}
        digest: ${{ steps.build.outputs.digest }}
    
    # 上传扫描结果
    - name: Upload Trivy results
      uses: github/codeql-action/upload-sarif@v2
      with:
        sarif_file: 'trivy-results.sarif'
```

#### 4. SBOM管理

**Syft生成SBOM**

```bash
#!/bin/bash
# generate-sbom.sh - 生成软件物料清单

# 安装Syft
install_syft() {
    curl -sSfL https://raw.githubusercontent.com/anchore/syft/main/install.sh | sh -s -- -b /usr/local/bin
}

# 生成镜像SBOM
generate_image_sbom() {
    local image=$1
    local format=${2:-spdx-json}
    local output="sbom-$(echo $image | tr '/:' '-')-$(date +%Y%m%d).${format##*-}"
    
    echo "生成镜像SBOM: $image"
    syft $image -o $format > $output
    
    echo "SBOM已保存到: $output"
}

# 生成目录SBOM
generate_dir_sbom() {
    local dir=$1
    local format=${2:-spdx-json}
    local output="sbom-$(basename $dir)-$(date +%Y%m%d).${format##*-}"
    
    echo "生成目录SBOM: $dir"
    syft dir:$dir -o $format > $output
    
    echo "SBOM已保存到: $output"
}

# 比较SBOM
compare_sbom() {
    local sbom1=$1
    local sbom2=$2
    
    echo "比较SBOM:"
    echo "  SBOM 1: $sbom1"
    echo "  SBOM 2: $sbom2"
    
    # 提取包列表
    jq -r '.packages[].name' $sbom1 | sort > /tmp/sbom1-packages.txt
    jq -r '.packages[].name' $sbom2 | sort > /tmp/sbom2-packages.txt
    
    # 显示差异
    echo -e "\n新增的包:"
    comm -13 /tmp/sbom1-packages.txt /tmp/sbom2-packages.txt
    
    echo -e "\n删除的包:"
    comm -23 /tmp/sbom1-packages.txt /tmp/sbom2-packages.txt
    
    echo -e "\n共同的包:"
    comm -12 /tmp/sbom1-packages.txt /tmp/sbom2-packages.txt | wc -l
}

# 验证SBOM
verify_sbom() {
    local sbom=$1
    
    echo "验证SBOM: $sbom"
    
    # 检查格式
    if jq empty $sbom 2>/dev/null; then
        echo "✓ SBOM格式有效"
    else
        echo "✗ SBOM格式无效"
        return 1
    fi
    
    # 检查必需字段
    local required_fields=("name" "version" "packages")
    for field in "${required_fields[@]}"; do
        if jq -e ".$field" $sbom > /dev/null 2>&1; then
            echo "✓ 字段 $field 存在"
        else
            echo "✗ 字段 $field 缺失"
            return 1
        fi
    done
    
    # 统计信息
    local package_count=$(jq '.packages | length' $sbom)
    echo "包数量: $package_count"
}

# 主函数
main() {
    case "$1" in
        image)
            if [ -z "$2" ]; then
                echo "用法: $0 image <image> [format]"
                exit 1
            fi
            generate_image_sbom "$2" "$3"
            ;;
        dir)
            if [ -z "$2" ]; then
                echo "用法: $0 dir <directory> [format]"
                exit 1
            fi
            generate_dir_sbom "$2" "$3"
            ;;
        compare)
            if [ -z "$3" ]; then
                echo "用法: $0 compare <sbom1> <sbom2>"
                exit 1
            fi
            compare_sbom "$2" "$3"
            ;;
        verify)
            if [ -z "$2" ]; then
                echo "用法: $0 verify <sbom>"
                exit 1
            fi
            verify_sbom "$2"
            ;;
        *)
            echo "用法: $0 {image|dir|compare|verify} [args]"
            exit 1
            ;;
    esac
}

main "$@"
```

**SBOM分析工具**

```go
// sbom-analyzer.go
package main

import (
    "encoding/json"
    "fmt"
    "log"
    "os"
    "sort"
)

// SBOM SPDX格式的SBOM结构
type SBOM struct {
    Name     string    `json:"name"`
    Version  string    `json:"version"`
    Packages []Package `json:"packages"`
}

// Package 包信息
type Package struct {
    Name             string   `json:"name"`
    Version          string   `json:"versionInfo"`
    Supplier         string   `json:"supplier"`
    DownloadLocation string   `json:"downloadLocation"`
    FilesAnalyzed    bool     `json:"filesAnalyzed"`
    LicenseConcluded string   `json:"licenseConcluded"`
    LicenseDeclared  string   `json:"licenseDeclared"`
    ExternalRefs     []ExtRef `json:"externalRefs"`
}

// ExtRef 外部引用
type ExtRef struct {
    Category string `json:"referenceCategory"`
    Type     string `json:"referenceType"`
    Locator  string `json:"referenceLocator"`
}

// SBOMAnalyzer SBOM分析器
type SBOMAnalyzer struct {
    sbom *SBOM
}

// NewSBOMAnalyzer 创建分析器
func NewSBOMAnalyzer(sbomFile string) (*SBOMAnalyzer, error) {
    data, err := os.ReadFile(sbomFile)
    if err != nil {
        return nil, err
    }
    
    var sbom SBOM
    if err := json.Unmarshal(data, &sbom); err != nil {
        return nil, err
    }
    
    return &SBOMAnalyzer{
        sbom: &sbom,
    }, nil
}

// AnalyzeLicenses 分析许可证
func (sa *SBOMAnalyzer) AnalyzeLicenses() {
    fmt.Println("=== 许可证分析 ===\n")
    
    licenses := make(map[string]int)
    
    for _, pkg := range sa.sbom.Packages {
        license := pkg.LicenseConcluded
        if license == "" {
            license = pkg.LicenseDeclared
        }
        if license == "" {
            license = "UNKNOWN"
        }
        licenses[license]++
    }
    
    // 排序并显示
    type kv struct {
        Key   string
        Value int
    }
    
    var sorted []kv
    for k, v := range licenses {
        sorted = append(sorted, kv{k, v})
    }
    
    sort.Slice(sorted, func(i, j int) bool {
        return sorted[i].Value > sorted[j].Value
    })
    
    for _, kv := range sorted {
        fmt.Printf("%-30s: %d\n", kv.Key, kv.Value)
    }
}

// FindVulnerablePackages 查找有漏洞的包
func (sa *SBOMAnalyzer) FindVulnerablePackages() {
    fmt.Println("\n=== 漏洞包检查 ===\n")
    
    // 这里简化处理,实际应该调用漏洞数据库API
    vulnerablePackages := []string{
        "log4j",
        "spring-core",
        "jackson-databind",
    }
    
    found := false
    for _, pkg := range sa.sbom.Packages {
        for _, vuln := range vulnerablePackages {
            if pkg.Name == vuln {
                fmt.Printf("⚠️  发现潜在漏洞包: %s@%s\n", pkg.Name, pkg.Version)
                found = true
            }
        }
    }
    
    if !found {
        fmt.Println("✓ 未发现已知漏洞包")
    }
}

// AnalyzeSuppliers 分析供应商
func (sa *SBOMAnalyzer) AnalyzeSuppliers() {
    fmt.Println("\n=== 供应商分析 ===\n")
    
    suppliers := make(map[string]int)
    
    for _, pkg := range sa.sbom.Packages {
        supplier := pkg.Supplier
        if supplier == "" {
            supplier = "UNKNOWN"
        }
        suppliers[supplier]++
    }
    
    // 排序并显示
    type kv struct {
        Key   string
        Value int
    }
    
    var sorted []kv
    for k, v := range suppliers {
        sorted = append(sorted, kv{k, v})
    }
    
    sort.Slice(sorted, func(i, j int) bool {
        return sorted[i].Value > sorted[j].Value
    })
    
    for _, kv := range sorted {
        fmt.Printf("%-50s: %d\n", kv.Key, kv.Value)
    }
}

// GenerateReport 生成报告
func (sa *SBOMAnalyzer) GenerateReport() {
    fmt.Println("========================================")
    fmt.Printf("SBOM分析报告: %s\n", sa.sbom.Name)
    fmt.Println("========================================\n")
    
    fmt.Printf("版本: %s\n", sa.sbom.Version)
    fmt.Printf("包数量: %d\n\n", len(sa.sbom.Packages))
    
    sa.AnalyzeLicenses()
    sa.FindVulnerablePackages()
    sa.AnalyzeSuppliers()
    
    fmt.Println("\n========================================")
    fmt.Println("分析完成")
    fmt.Println("========================================")
}

func main() {
    if len(os.Args) < 2 {
        log.Fatal("用法: sbom-analyzer <sbom-file>")
    }
    
    analyzer, err := NewSBOMAnalyzer(os.Args[1])
    if err != nil {
        log.Fatalf("加载SBOM失败: %v", err)
    }
    
    analyzer.GenerateReport()
}
```

**镜像策略控制器**

```yaml
# image-policy-webhook.yaml
apiVersion: v1
kind: ConfigMap
metadata:
  name: image-policy-webhook
  namespace: kube-system
data:
  policy.yaml: |
    # 镜像策略配置
    imagePolicy:
      # 允许的镜像仓库
      allowedRegistries:
        - registry.example.com
        - gcr.io/my-project
        - quay.io/my-org
      
      # 拒绝的镜像仓库
      deniedRegistries:
        - docker.io  # 禁止使用Docker Hub
      
      # 要求镜像签名
      requireSignature: true
      
      # 要求SBOM
      requireSBOM: true
      
      # 最大镜像年龄(天)
      maxImageAge: 90
      
      # 禁止的标签
      deniedTags:
        - latest
        - dev
        - test
      
      # 漏洞扫描要求
      vulnerabilityPolicy:
        maxCritical: 0
        maxHigh: 5
        maxMedium: 20
      
      # 许可证白名单
      allowedLicenses:
        - MIT
        - Apache-2.0
        - BSD-3-Clause
        - ISC
      
      # 许可证黑名单
      deniedLicenses:
        - GPL-3.0
        - AGPL-3.0
```



### 10.4.5 运行时安全

#### 1. 容器运行时安全

**gVisor沙箱运行时**

```yaml
# gvisor-runtimeclass.yaml
apiVersion: node.k8s.io/v1
kind: RuntimeClass
metadata:
  name: gvisor
handler: runsc
---
# 使用gVisor运行Pod
apiVersion: v1
kind: Pod
metadata:
  name: secure-pod
spec:
  runtimeClassName: gvisor
  containers:
  - name: app
    image: nginx:alpine
    securityContext:
      runAsNonRoot: true
      runAsUser: 1000
      allowPrivilegeEscalation: false
      capabilities:
        drop:
        - ALL
      readOnlyRootFilesystem: true
```

overhead:

**AppArmor配置**

```yaml
# apparmor-profile.yaml
apiVersion: v1
kind: ConfigMap
metadata:
  name: apparmor-profile
  namespace: security
data:
  nginx-profile: |
    #include <tunables/global>
    
    profile k8s-nginx flags=(attach_disconnected,mediate_deleted) {
      #include <abstractions/base>
      
      # 允许网络访问
      network inet tcp,
      network inet udp,
      network inet6 tcp,
      network inet6 udp,
      
      # 允许文件访问
      /usr/sbin/nginx ix,
      /etc/nginx/** r,
      /var/log/nginx/** w,
      /var/cache/nginx/** rw,
      /run/nginx.pid rw,
      
      # 允许临时文件
      /tmp/** rw,
      
      # 拒绝其他所有访问
      deny /** wx,
    }
---
# 使用AppArmor的Pod
apiVersion: v1
kind: Pod
metadata:
  name: apparmor-pod
  annotations:
    container.apparmor.security.beta.kubernetes.io/nginx: localhost/k8s-nginx
spec:
  containers:
  - name: nginx
    image: nginx:alpine
```

#### 2. 运行时威胁检测

**Falco规则配置**

```yaml
# falco-rules.yaml
- rule: Unauthorized Process
  desc: Detect unauthorized process execution
  condition: >
    spawned_process and
    not proc.name in (allowed_processes)
  output: >
    Unauthorized process started
    (user=%user.name command=%proc.cmdline
    container=%container.name image=%container.image.repository)
  priority: WARNING
  tags: [process, container]

- rule: Write below root
  desc: Detect writes below root directory
  condition: >
    write and
    fd.name startswith "/" and
    not fd.name startswith "/tmp" and
    not fd.name startswith "/var"
  output: >
    File write below root
    (user=%user.name command=%proc.cmdline
    file=%fd.name container=%container.name)
  priority: ERROR
  tags: [filesystem, container]

- rule: Container Drift Detected
  desc: Detect container drift (file modifications)
  condition: >
    container and
    not container.image.repository in (allowed_images) and
    (modify or rename or unlink)
  output: >
    Container drift detected
    (user=%user.name command=%proc.cmdline
    file=%fd.name container=%container.name)
  priority: WARNING
  tags: [container, drift]

- rule: Reverse Shell
  desc: Detect reverse shell connections
  condition: >
    spawned_process and
    (proc.name in (shell_binaries) and
    (proc.args contains "-i" or
     proc.args contains "/dev/tcp" or
     proc.args contains "/dev/udp" or
     proc.args contains ">&" or
     proc.args contains "2>&"))
  output: >
    Reverse shell detected
    (user=%user.name command=%proc.cmdline
    connection=%fd.name container=%container.name)
  priority: CRITICAL
  tags: [network, shell]

- rule: Crypto Mining
  desc: Detect cryptocurrency mining activity
  condition: >
    spawned_process and
    (proc.name in (crypto_miners) or
     proc.cmdline contains "stratum" or
     proc.cmdline contains "xmrig" or
     proc.cmdline contains "minerd")
  output: >
    Crypto mining detected
    (user=%user.name command=%proc.cmdline
    container=%container.name)
  priority: CRITICAL
  tags: [process, mining]
```

**Falco Sidekick集成**

```yaml
# falco-sidekick.yaml
apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: Deployment
metadata:
  name: falco-sidekick
  namespace: falco
spec:
  replicas: 2
  selector:
    matchLabels:
      app: falco-sidekick
  template:
    metadata:
      labels:
        app: falco-sidekick
    spec:
      containers:
      - name: falco-sidekick
        image: falcosecurity/falcosidekick:latest
        ports:
        - containerPort: 2801
        env:
        # Slack通知
        - name: SLACK_WEBHOOKURL
          valueFrom:
            secretKeyRef:
              name: falco-sidekick-secrets
              key: slack-webhook
        - name: SLACK_MINIMUMPRIORITY
          value: "warning"
        
        # Elasticsearch输出
        - name: ELASTICSEARCH_HOSTPORT
          value: "elasticsearch:9200"
        - name: ELASTICSEARCH_INDEX
          value: "falco"
        - name: ELASTICSEARCH_TYPE
          value: "_doc"
        
        # Prometheus metrics
        - name: PROMETHEUS_EXTRALABELS
          value: "cluster:production"
        
        # Webhook输出
        - name: WEBHOOK_ADDRESS
          value: "http://alert-manager:9093/api/v1/alerts"
        
        resources:
          requests:
            cpu: 100m
            memory: 128Mi
          limits:
            cpu: 500m
            memory: 512Mi
```

#### 3. 容器逃逸防护

**容器安全上下文最佳实践**

```yaml
# secure-pod-template.yaml
apiVersion: v1
kind: Pod
metadata:
  name: secure-app
spec:
  # Pod级别安全上下文
  securityContext:
    runAsNonRoot: true
    runAsUser: 1000
    runAsGroup: 3000
    fsGroup: 2000
    fsGroupChangePolicy: "OnRootMismatch"
    seccompProfile:
      type: RuntimeDefault
    supplementalGroups: [4000]
  
  containers:
  - name: app
    image: myapp:v1.0
    
    # 容器级别安全上下文
    securityContext:
      allowPrivilegeEscalation: false
      readOnlyRootFilesystem: true
      runAsNonRoot: true
      runAsUser: 1000
      capabilities:
        drop:
        - ALL
        add:
        - NET_BIND_SERVICE
      seccompProfile:
        type: RuntimeDefault
    
    # 资源限制
    resources:
      requests:
        cpu: 100m
        memory: 128Mi
      limits:
        cpu: 500m
        memory: 512Mi
    
    # 只读根文件系统需要临时目录
    volumeMounts:
    - name: tmp
      mountPath: /tmp
    - name: cache
      mountPath: /app/cache
  
  volumes:
  - name: tmp
    emptyDir: {}
  - name: cache
    emptyDir: {}
```

**OPA Gatekeeper约束**

```yaml
# gatekeeper-constraints.yaml
# 禁止特权容器
apiVersion: constraints.gatekeeper.sh/v1beta1
kind: K8sPSPPrivilegedContainer
metadata:
  name: psp-privileged-container
spec:
  match:
    kinds:
    - apiGroups: [""]
      kinds: ["Pod"]
    excludedNamespaces:
    - kube-system
---
# 要求只读根文件系统
apiVersion: constraints.gatekeeper.sh/v1beta1
kind: K8sPSPReadOnlyRootFilesystem
metadata:
  name: psp-readonlyrootfilesystem
spec:
  match:
    kinds:
    - apiGroups: [""]
      kinds: ["Pod"]
---
# 禁止hostPath卷
apiVersion: constraints.gatekeeper.sh/v1beta1
kind: K8sPSPHostFilesystem
metadata:
  name: psp-host-filesystem
spec:
  match:
    kinds:
    - apiGroups: [""]
      kinds: ["Pod"]
  parameters:
    allowedHostPaths: []
---
# 要求非root用户
apiVersion: constraints.gatekeeper.sh/v1beta1
kind: K8sPSPAllowedUsers
metadata:
  name: psp-pods-must-run-as-nonroot
spec:
  match:
    kinds:
    - apiGroups: [""]
      kinds: ["Pod"]
  parameters:
    runAsUser:
      rule: MustRunAsNonRoot
---
# 限制capabilities
apiVersion: constraints.gatekeeper.sh/v1beta1
kind: K8sPSPCapabilities
metadata:
  name: psp-capabilities
spec:
  match:
    kinds:
    - apiGroups: [""]
      kinds: ["Pod"]
  parameters:
    allowedCapabilities: []
    requiredDropCapabilities:
    - ALL
```



### 10.4.6 合规性管理

#### 1. 合规框架

**PCI DSS合规配置**

```yaml
# pci-dss-compliance.yaml
# PCI DSS要求的安全配置
apiVersion: v1
kind: ConfigMap
metadata:
  name: pci-dss-requirements
  namespace: compliance
data:
  requirements.yaml: |
    # PCI DSS 4.0主要要求
    requirements:
      # 要求1: 安装和维护网络安全控制
      - id: "1"
        controls:
          - "实施网络分段"
          - "配置防火墙规则"
          - "限制入站和出站流量"
        kubernetes_implementation:
          - "NetworkPolicy"
          - "Calico/Cilium策略"
          - "Ingress/Egress控制"
      
      # 要求2: 应用安全配置
      - id: "2"
        controls:
          - "更改默认密码"
          - "禁用不必要的服务"
          - "加密管理访问"
        kubernetes_implementation:
          - "Secret管理"
          - "RBAC最小权限"
          - "TLS加密"
      
      # 要求3: 保护存储的账户数据
      - id: "3"
        controls:
          - "数据加密"
          - "密钥管理"
          - "数据保留策略"
        kubernetes_implementation:
          - "etcd加密"
          - "Volume加密"
          - "KMS集成"
      
      # 要求4: 通过公共网络传输时保护账户数据
      - id: "4"
        controls:
          - "强加密协议"
          - "TLS 1.2+"
          - "证书管理"
        kubernetes_implementation:
          - "Ingress TLS"
          - "Service Mesh mTLS"
          - "cert-manager"
      
      # 要求5: 保护所有系统免受恶意软件侵害
      - id: "5"
        controls:
          - "防病毒软件"
          - "恶意软件检测"
          - "定期扫描"
        kubernetes_implementation:
          - "镜像扫描"
          - "运行时检测"
          - "Falco规则"
      
      # 要求6: 开发和维护安全系统和软件
      - id: "6"
        controls:
          - "安全开发流程"
          - "漏洞管理"
          - "变更控制"
        kubernetes_implementation:
          - "CI/CD安全"
          - "镜像签名"
          - "GitOps"
      
      # 要求7: 限制对账户数据的访问
      - id: "7"
        controls:
          - "最小权限原则"
          - "访问控制"
          - "权限审查"
        kubernetes_implementation:
          - "RBAC"
          - "Pod Security"
          - "准入控制"
      
      # 要求8: 识别用户和验证对系统组件的访问
      - id: "8"
        controls:
          - "唯一ID"
          - "强认证"
          - "MFA"
        kubernetes_implementation:
          - "OIDC集成"
          - "ServiceAccount"
          - "证书认证"
      
      # 要求9: 限制对账户数据的物理访问
      - id: "9"
        controls:
          - "物理访问控制"
          - "设备安全"
          - "介质销毁"
        kubernetes_implementation:
          - "云提供商合规"
          - "节点安全"
          - "数据销毁策略"
      
      # 要求10: 记录和监控所有对系统组件和账户数据的访问
      - id: "10"
        controls:
          - "审计日志"
          - "日志保护"
          - "日志审查"
        kubernetes_implementation:
          - "审计日志"
          - "日志聚合"
          - "SIEM集成"
      
      # 要求11: 定期测试安全系统和流程
      - id: "11"
        controls:
          - "漏洞扫描"
          - "渗透测试"
          - "入侵检测"
        kubernetes_implementation:
          - "定期扫描"
          - "混沌工程"
          - "Falco检测"
      
      # 要求12: 支持信息安全政策
      - id: "12"
        controls:
          - "安全政策"
          - "风险评估"
          - "安全意识培训"
        kubernetes_implementation:
          - "策略即代码"
          - "合规自动化"
          - "文档管理"
```

#### 2. 合规自动化

**Open Policy Agent (OPA)策略**

```rego
# compliance-policies.rego
package kubernetes.admission

# 拒绝没有资源限制的Pod
deny[msg] {
    input.request.kind.kind == "Pod"
    container := input.request.object.spec.containers[_]
    not container.resources.limits
    msg := sprintf("容器 %v 必须设置资源限制", [container.name])
}

# 要求所有镜像来自允许的仓库
deny[msg] {
    input.request.kind.kind == "Pod"
    container := input.request.object.spec.containers[_]
    image := container.image
    not startswith(image, "registry.example.com/")
    msg := sprintf("镜像 %v 必须来自允许的仓库", [image])
}

# 禁止特权容器
deny[msg] {
    input.request.kind.kind == "Pod"
    container := input.request.object.spec.containers[_]
    container.securityContext.privileged == true
    msg := sprintf("容器 %v 不能使用特权模式", [container.name])
}

# 要求非root用户
deny[msg] {
    input.request.kind.kind == "Pod"
    not input.request.object.spec.securityContext.runAsNonRoot
    msg := "Pod必须以非root用户运行"
}

# 要求只读根文件系统
deny[msg] {
    input.request.kind.kind == "Pod"
    container := input.request.object.spec.containers[_]
    not container.securityContext.readOnlyRootFilesystem
    msg := sprintf("容器 %v 必须使用只读根文件系统", [container.name])
}

# 禁止hostNetwork
deny[msg] {
    input.request.kind.kind == "Pod"
    input.request.object.spec.hostNetwork == true
    msg := "Pod不能使用hostNetwork"
}

# 要求标签
deny[msg] {
    input.request.kind.kind == "Pod"
    required_labels := {"app", "version", "owner"}
    provided_labels := {label | input.request.object.metadata.labels[label]}
    missing_labels := required_labels - provided_labels
    count(missing_labels) > 0
    msg := sprintf("Pod缺少必需的标签: %v", [missing_labels])
}

# 审计日志记录
audit[msg] {
    input.request.kind.kind == "Pod"
    msg := {
        "action": "pod_created",
        "user": input.request.userInfo.username,
        "namespace": input.request.namespace,
        "pod": input.request.object.metadata.name,
        "timestamp": time.now_ns()
    }
}
```

**合规扫描工具**

```bash
#!/bin/bash
# compliance-scan.sh - 合规性扫描

# 使用kube-bench扫描CIS基准
scan_cis_benchmark() {
    echo "=== CIS Kubernetes Benchmark扫描 ==="
    
    kubectl apply -f - <<EOF
apiVersion: batch/v1
kind: Job
metadata:
  name: kube-bench
  namespace: default
spec:
  template:
    spec:
      hostPID: true
      containers:
      - name: kube-bench
        image: aquasec/kube-bench:latest
        command: ["kube-bench"]
        volumeMounts:
        - name: var-lib-etcd
          mountPath: /var/lib/etcd
          readOnly: true
        - name: var-lib-kubelet
          mountPath: /var/lib/kubelet
          readOnly: true
        - name: etc-systemd
          mountPath: /etc/systemd
          readOnly: true
        - name: etc-kubernetes
          mountPath: /etc/kubernetes
          readOnly: true
      restartPolicy: Never
      volumes:
      - name: var-lib-etcd
        hostPath:
          path: "/var/lib/etcd"
      - name: var-lib-kubelet
        hostPath:
          path: "/var/lib/kubelet"
      - name: etc-systemd
        hostPath:
          path: "/etc/systemd"
      - name: etc-kubernetes
        hostPath:
          path: "/etc/kubernetes"
EOF
    
    # 等待Job完成
    kubectl wait --for=condition=complete --timeout=300s job/kube-bench
    
    # 获取结果
    kubectl logs job/kube-bench
    
    # 清理
    kubectl delete job kube-bench
}

# 使用kubescape扫描
scan_kubescape() {
    echo "=== Kubescape安全扫描 ==="
    
    # 安装kubescape
    curl -s https://raw.githubusercontent.com/kubescape/kubescape/master/install.sh | /bin/bash
    
    # 扫描集群
    kubescape scan framework nsa,mitre --exclude-namespaces kube-system,kube-public
    
    # 生成HTML报告
    kubescape scan framework nsa --format html --output kubescape-report.html
    
    echo "报告已保存到: kubescape-report.html"
}

# 使用Polaris扫描
scan_polaris() {
    echo "=== Polaris配置验证 ==="
    
    kubectl apply -f https://github.com/FairwindsOps/polaris/releases/latest/download/dashboard.yaml
    
    echo "Polaris Dashboard已部署"
    echo "访问: kubectl port-forward --namespace polaris svc/polaris-dashboard 8080:80"
}

# 主函数
main() {
    case "$1" in
        cis)
            scan_cis_benchmark
            ;;
        kubescape)
            scan_kubescape
            ;;
        polaris)
            scan_polaris
            ;;
        all)
            scan_cis_benchmark
            scan_kubescape
            scan_polaris
            ;;
        *)
            echo "用法: $0 {cis|kubescape|polaris|all}"
            exit 1
            ;;
    esac
}

main "$@"
```

#### 3. 审计与报告

**审计日志策略**

```yaml
# audit-policy.yaml
apiVersion: audit.k8s.io/v1
kind: Policy
rules:
# 不记录只读请求
- level: None
  verbs: ["get", "list", "watch"]

# 记录Secret的元数据
- level: Metadata
  resources:
  - group: ""
    resources: ["secrets"]

# 记录ConfigMap的元数据
- level: Metadata
  resources:
  - group: ""
    resources: ["configmaps"]

# 记录所有认证请求
- level: RequestResponse
  verbs: ["create", "update", "patch", "delete"]
  resources:
  - group: "authentication.k8s.io"

# 记录所有授权请求
- level: RequestResponse
  verbs: ["create", "update", "patch", "delete"]
  resources:
  - group: "authorization.k8s.io"

# 记录RBAC变更
- level: RequestResponse
  verbs: ["create", "update", "patch", "delete"]
  resources:
  - group: "rbac.authorization.k8s.io"

# 记录Pod创建和删除
- level: Request
  verbs: ["create", "delete"]
  resources:
  - group: ""
    resources: ["pods"]

# 记录Service变更
- level: Request
  verbs: ["create", "update", "patch", "delete"]
  resources:
  - group: ""
    resources: ["services"]

# 记录Ingress变更
- level: Request
  verbs: ["create", "update", "patch", "delete"]
  resources:
  - group: "networking.k8s.io"
    resources: ["ingresses"]

# 记录PersistentVolume操作
- level: Request
  verbs: ["create", "update", "patch", "delete"]
  resources:
  - group: ""
    resources: ["persistentvolumes", "persistentvolumeclaims"]

# 默认记录元数据
- level: Metadata
```

**合规报告生成器**

```go
// compliance-reporter.go
package main

import (
    "context"
    "fmt"
    "log"
    "time"
    
    metav1 "k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/apis/meta/v1"
    "k8s.io/client-go/kubernetes"
    "k8s.io/client-go/rest"
)

// ComplianceReporter 合规报告生成器
type ComplianceReporter struct {
    clientset *kubernetes.Clientset
}

// NewComplianceReporter 创建报告生成器
func NewComplianceReporter() (*ComplianceReporter, error) {
    config, err := rest.InClusterConfig()
    if err != nil {
        return nil, err
    }
    
    clientset, err := kubernetes.NewForConfig(config)
    if err != nil {
        return nil, err
    }
    
    return &ComplianceReporter{
        clientset: clientset,
    }, nil
}

// GenerateReport 生成合规报告
func (cr *ComplianceReporter) GenerateReport(ctx context.Context) error {
    fmt.Println("========================================")
    fmt.Println("Kubernetes合规性报告")
    fmt.Printf("生成时间: %s\n", time.Now().Format("2006-01-02 15:04:05"))
    fmt.Println("========================================\n")
    
    // 1. 集群信息
    if err := cr.reportClusterInfo(ctx); err != nil {
        return err
    }
    
    // 2. 安全配置
    if err := cr.reportSecurityConfig(ctx); err != nil {
        return err
    }
    
    // 3. RBAC配置
    if err := cr.reportRBACConfig(ctx); err != nil {
        return err
    }
    
    // 4. 网络策略
    if err := cr.reportNetworkPolicies(ctx); err != nil {
        return err
    }
    
    // 5. Pod安全
    if err := cr.reportPodSecurity(ctx); err != nil {
        return err
    }
    
    // 6. 审计日志
    if err := cr.reportAuditLogs(ctx); err != nil {
        return err
    }
    
    fmt.Println("\n========================================")
    fmt.Println("报告生成完成")
    fmt.Println("========================================")
    
    return nil
}

// reportClusterInfo 报告集群信息
func (cr *ComplianceReporter) reportClusterInfo(ctx context.Context) error {
    fmt.Println("=== 集群信息 ===\n")
    
    // 获取节点信息
    nodes, err := cr.clientset.CoreV1().Nodes().List(ctx, metav1.ListOptions{})
    if err != nil {
        return err
    }
    
    fmt.Printf("节点数量: %d\n", len(nodes.Items))
    
    // 获取命名空间
    namespaces, err := cr.clientset.CoreV1().Namespaces().List(ctx, metav1.ListOptions{})
    if err != nil {
        return err
    }
    
    fmt.Printf("命名空间数量: %d\n", len(namespaces.Items))
    
    // 获取Pod数量
    pods, err := cr.clientset.CoreV1().Pods("").List(ctx, metav1.ListOptions{})
    if err != nil {
        return err
    }
    
    fmt.Printf("Pod总数: %d\n", len(pods.Items))
    
    return nil
}

// reportSecurityConfig 报告安全配置
func (cr *ComplianceReporter) reportSecurityConfig(ctx context.Context) error {
    fmt.Println("\n=== 安全配置 ===\n")
    
    // 检查PSP
    psps, err := cr.clientset.PolicyV1beta1().PodSecurityPolicies().List(ctx, metav1.ListOptions{})
    if err == nil {
        fmt.Printf("Pod安全策略数量: %d\n", len(psps.Items))
    }
    
    // 检查NetworkPolicy
    nps, err := cr.clientset.NetworkingV1().NetworkPolicies("").List(ctx, metav1.ListOptions{})
    if err == nil {
        fmt.Printf("网络策略数量: %d\n", len(nps.Items))
    }
    
    return nil
}

// reportRBACConfig 报告RBAC配置
func (cr *ComplianceReporter) reportRBACConfig(ctx context.Context) error {
    fmt.Println("\n=== RBAC配置 ===\n")
    
    // ClusterRole
    clusterRoles, err := cr.clientset.RbacV1().ClusterRoles().List(ctx, metav1.ListOptions{})
    if err != nil {
        return err
    }
    fmt.Printf("ClusterRole数量: %d\n", len(clusterRoles.Items))
    
    // ClusterRoleBinding
    clusterRoleBindings, err := cr.clientset.RbacV1().ClusterRoleBindings().List(ctx, metav1.ListOptions{})
    if err != nil {
        return err
    }
    fmt.Printf("ClusterRoleBinding数量: %d\n", len(clusterRoleBindings.Items))
    
    // Role
    roles, err := cr.clientset.RbacV1().Roles("").List(ctx, metav1.ListOptions{})
    if err != nil {
        return err
    }
    fmt.Printf("Role数量: %d\n", len(roles.Items))
    
    // RoleBinding
    roleBindings, err := cr.clientset.RbacV1().RoleBindings("").List(ctx, metav1.ListOptions{})
    if err != nil {
        return err
    }
    fmt.Printf("RoleBinding数量: %d\n", len(roleBindings.Items))
    
    return nil
}

// reportNetworkPolicies 报告网络策略
func (cr *ComplianceReporter) reportNetworkPolicies(ctx context.Context) error {
    fmt.Println("\n=== 网络策略 ===\n")
    
    nps, err := cr.clientset.NetworkingV1().NetworkPolicies("").List(ctx, metav1.ListOptions{})
    if err != nil {
        return err
    }
    
    if len(nps.Items) == 0 {
        fmt.Println("⚠️  未配置网络策略")
        return nil
    }
    
    // 按命名空间统计
    nsByNs := make(map[string]int)
    for _, np := range nps.Items {
        nsByNs[np.Namespace]++
    }
    
    fmt.Println("按命名空间统计:")
    for ns, count := range nsByNs {
        fmt.Printf("  %s: %d\n", ns, count)
    }
    
    return nil
}

// reportPodSecurity 报告Pod安全
func (cr *ComplianceReporter) reportPodSecurity(ctx context.Context) error {
    fmt.Println("\n=== Pod安全 ===\n")
    
    pods, err := cr.clientset.CoreV1().Pods("").List(ctx, metav1.ListOptions{})
    if err != nil {
        return err
    }
    
    privilegedCount := 0
    hostNetworkCount := 0
    noResourceLimitsCount := 0
    
    for _, pod := range pods.Items {
        // 检查特权容器
        for _, container := range pod.Spec.Containers {
            if container.SecurityContext != nil &&
               container.SecurityContext.Privileged != nil &&
               *container.SecurityContext.Privileged {
                privilegedCount++
            }
            
            // 检查资源限制
            if container.Resources.Limits == nil {
                noResourceLimitsCount++
            }
        }
        
        // 检查hostNetwork
        if pod.Spec.HostNetwork {
            hostNetworkCount++
        }
    }
    
    fmt.Printf("特权容器数量: %d\n", privilegedCount)
    fmt.Printf("使用hostNetwork的Pod: %d\n", hostNetworkCount)
    fmt.Printf("未设置资源限制的容器: %d\n", noResourceLimitsCount)
    
    if privilegedCount > 0 {
        fmt.Println("⚠️  发现特权容器")
    }
    if hostNetworkCount > 0 {
        fmt.Println("⚠️  发现使用hostNetwork的Pod")
    }
    if noResourceLimitsCount > 0 {
        fmt.Println("⚠️  发现未设置资源限制的容器")
    }
    
    return nil
}

// reportAuditLogs 报告审计日志
func (cr *ComplianceReporter) reportAuditLogs(ctx context.Context) error {
    fmt.Println("\n=== 审计日志 ===\n")
    
    // 这里简化处理,实际应该查询审计日志系统
    fmt.Println("审计日志配置: 已启用")
    fmt.Println("日志保留期: 90天")
    fmt.Println("日志存储: Elasticsearch")
    
    return nil
}

func main() {
    reporter, err := NewComplianceReporter()
    if err != nil {
        log.Fatalf("创建报告生成器失败: %v", err)
    }
    
    ctx := context.Background()
    if err := reporter.GenerateReport(ctx); err != nil {
        log.Fatalf("生成报告失败: %v", err)
    }
}
```

---

**本节小结**

安全加固与合规性是Kubernetes生产环境的基石。通过实施多层次的安全控制、自动化的合规检查和持续的安全监控,可以构建一个安全可靠的容器平台。关键要点包括:

1. **纵深防御**: 采用4C安全模型,在云、集群、容器和代码层面实施安全控制
2. **身份与访问**: 实施强认证、细粒度授权和最小权限原则
3. **网络安全**: 使用网络策略、服务网格和加密通信保护数据传输
4. **供应链安全**: 通过镜像扫描、签名验证和SBOM管理确保软件供应链安全
5. **运行时保护**: 使用沙箱运行时、安全上下文和威胁检测防止容器逃逸
6. **合规自动化**: 通过策略即代码和自动化扫描确保持续合规

安全是一个持续的过程,需要定期评估、测试和改进安全措施,以应对不断演变的威胁。
